  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_9ea16cc7-027e-44d0-b0ca-25e339c8aa49'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText16517397711102261090" style="display:none">A heart to protect. A debt to repay. A game to win.<br /><br />After being swept up in the magical world of Caraval, Donatella Dragna has finally escaped her father and saved her sister, Scarlett, from a disastrous arranged marriage. The girls should be celebrating, but Tella isn’t yet free. She made a desperate bargain with a mysterious criminal, and what Tella owes him no one has ever been able to deliver: Caraval Master Legend’s true name.<br /><br />The only chance of uncovering Legend’s identity is to win Caraval, so Tella throws herself into the legendary competition once more—and into the path of the murderous heir to the throne, a doomed love story, and a web of secrets…including her sister's. Caraval has always demanded bravery, cunning, and sacrifice, but now the game is asking for more. If Tella can’t fulfill her bargain and deliver Legend’s name, she’ll lose everything she cares about—maybe even her life. But if she wins, Legend and Caraval will be destroyed forever...<br /><br /><b>Welcome, welcome to Caraval . . . the games have only just begun.</b></span>

  <span id="freeText2963363432956985976" style="display:none">Deal alert (12/29): I don't know how long this is going to last, but for the first time ever the Legendary ebook is on sale for only $2.99 (across all platforms). If you've been wanting to pick up the book, or get into this series, now is a great time! <br /><br />Hey friends! <br />Updating this to thank everyone who wrote in Legendary for the Goodreads Choice awards. I was so grateful and excited when I woke up this morning and saw that it had made e it into the Semifinal Round!! You are all the best!! <br /><br />Legendary is out today!! I'm so excited for readers to jump into this story! I hope you all enjoy it!<br /><br />May 23rd Update: Legendary is only six days away! I'm so excited, and for anyone else who might be excited too, I thought it would be fun to share my Legendary Pinterest Board: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.pinterest.com/stephaniegarber/legendary-a-caraval-novel/">https://www.pinterest.com/stephaniega...</a><br /><br />Another update: Lots of readers have been asking me if Legendary is the last book in the Caraval series or if there will be more, and I'm thrilled to share that there will be another book: FINALE. I'm so excited to write this book, and if you're interested you can add it to your Goodreads shelf right now: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/39071288-finale">https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3...</a><br /><br />Update March 19, 2018: More exciting news! I'm going on tour for Legendary and today Bustle announced tour dates and locations. Hope to see some of you there: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.bustle.com/p/caraval-legendary-author-stephanie-garber-is-going-on-tour-you-can-read-excerpt-from-her-new-book-now-8534977">https://www.bustle.com/p/caraval-lege...</a></span>

<div id="review_1918649764" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1918649764" />
    <a title="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink"><img alt="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568991289p2/50044222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1918649764?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" href="/user/show/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink">Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781250095336" href="/book/show/33645809-legendary">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=2018-anticipated-reads">2018-anticipated-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=favorite-villians">favorite-villians</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=recommended-fantasy">recommended-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=arcs-i-ve-reviewed">arcs-i-ve-reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=favorite-heroines">favorite-heroines</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1918649764" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15846069421536761338">Oh. Ohhhh.<br/><br/>I devoured this wonderful, torturous book. And now I don't know what to do with myself aside from sit here and try and form some semblance of a review.<br/><br/><b>Friends, if you think you know everything about Caraval, you'd be wrong.</b><br/><br/>I'm going to keep this review spoiler free, especially as we're a little ways away from the release, but I'll just say this took a verrrry unexpected turn and I couldn't be more thrilled. But a word to the wise (and for those who know me) - I like when books throw pu</span>
  <span id="freeText15846069421536761338" style="display:none">Oh. Ohhhh.<br><br>I devoured this wonderful, torturous book. And now I don't know what to do with myself aside from sit here and try and form some semblance of a review.<br><br><b>Friends, if you think you know everything about Caraval, you'd be wrong.</b><br><br>I'm going to keep this review spoiler free, especially as we're a little ways away from the release, but I'll just say this took a verrrry unexpected turn and I couldn't be more thrilled. But a word to the wise (and for those who know me) - I like when books throw punches in your gut and make you doubt everything you thought you knew. <br><br><i>First... a HUGE thank you to the amazing author, Stephanie, for the MS. I can't even begin to express my gratitude!</i><br><br>Legendary is told from Tella's perspective, and much to my delight, it picked up the morning after the first book. We're thrown into Tella's world and the consequences she faces after Caraval. And oh, there are plenty. I won't say much, but she owes a debt to a certain someone, and she's quickly swept up in a battle between power players. <br><br>Let's just say... Legend has enemies. Someone wants his true identity unmasked, and if Tella doesn't discover him and hand him over, she'll face losing everything, including her own life.<br><br>I knew I would like Tella, especially after what she did in the first book, but I didn't expect to fall so head-over-heels for this girl. She's way more complex and brave than she lets on. This is a girl you can root for. There's much more to her history and past that you don't get from Scarlett's POV, and oh my heart broke for her over and over. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>This was why love was so dangerous. Love turned the world into a garden, so beguiling it was easy to forget that rose petals were as ephemeral as feelings, eventually they would wilt and die, leaving nothing but the thorns.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>But perhaps the second best part was the returning characters. Though we're in Tella's POV, not even Scarlett's story is finished. She and Julian are still around, and so are rest of the Caraval crew. And of course, we're introduced to a new ensemble of characters.<br><br>And an entirely new world.<br><br>In fact, I daresay this one is even more magical than the last. New settings, new myths come to life. I will say it still felt a bit abstract, which certainly isn't a bad thing, especially if you like to get lost in your own imagination. The world is limitless here, and there be monsters. <br><br>Very dashing monsters, at that. Did I mention this book was hooooot? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517516049ra/24983860.gif" width="300px" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For anyone that followed my status updates (and there were plenty - I couldn't help myself...) I was going straight up bananas. Like, let me tell you right now, you are in for a ride. Much like my experience of the first book, I was literally freaaaking out coming up with new theories around every corner. In this, oh my goodness... I can't even talk about it. <br><br>IS IT REALLY A GAME? OR IS IT REAL THIS TIME? AHHHHH.<br><br>In fact, I was worried about the ending. There was sooo much intrigue and so many open plots and there was no way it could live up. <br><br>But, oh... the end was beautiful. Because I had a billion and a half theories, I won't answer whether or not I was surprised. I will say this: Legend's reveal was perfection, and now I need to reread the whole series just to fully comprehend everything that took place.<br><br>But even still, I found myself even wanting more. Then I asked myself <i>why</i>. Why did I want more? <br><br>The answer was simple. <br><br>I just couldn’t bear to leave the world or the characters. I didn't want it to be over. <br><br>My advice to you is this: Go into this with no expectations and simply get lost with Tella. Just enjoy the ride, the characters, the thrill of adventure. There's a lot to wrap up in this book, and while I wanted to stay forever and learn everything about everyone, I am so in love with the end. <br><br>Stephanie crafted it perfectly.<br><br><a href="http://www.herbookishthings.com" rel="nofollow noopener">My Blog</a> ~ <a href="https://www.instagram.com/reverieandink/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ~ <a href="https://twitter.com/reverieandink" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ~ <a href="https://www.etsy.com/shop/reverieandink" rel="nofollow noopener">Etsy</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15846069421536761338" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2368889292" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2368889292" />
    <a title="Cristina Monica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica"><img alt="Cristina Monica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589617514p2/14596170.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2368889292?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristina Monica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristina Monica" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica">Cristina Monica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=kill-me-now-slow-paced">kill-me-now-slow-paced</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=alpha-males">alpha-males</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=siblings">siblings</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2368889292" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9601171577469361176"><b>The magic is gone.</b><br/><br/>I don’t know where it went. I wish I could go on an adventure to find it, but alas I have finals next week. <br/><br/><i>Caraval</i> was one of my top five favourite releases of 2017. I remember when I received my copy of it, I took tons of pictures and kept staring at it like I was drunk with love.<br/><br/>That one was fast-paced and action-packed and so very surprising as well as enchanting. Legendary is <u>none</u> of those things.<br/><br/>It’s slow-paced, character-driven, mostly predictable and basically magic-les</span>
  <span id="freeText9601171577469361176" style="display:none"><b>The magic is gone.</b><br /><br />I don’t know where it went. I wish I could go on an adventure to find it, but alas I have finals next week. <br /><br /><i>Caraval</i> was one of my top five favourite releases of 2017. I remember when I received my copy of it, I took tons of pictures and kept staring at it like I was drunk with love.<br /><br />That one was fast-paced and action-packed and so very surprising as well as enchanting. Legendary is <u>none</u> of those things.<br /><br />It’s slow-paced, character-driven, mostly predictable and basically magic-less. All of those things would have been somewhat acceptable if the characters had been keepers.<br /><br />They’re not. Tella is an authentic woman, which I quite like about her. She is unapologetic about her arguably bad choices in men and she walks with her head held high. <br /><br />But she’s not smart. She may admit to being that, and show pride in it, but the number of mistakes she makes is ridiculous. One time, she actually wastes a question asking a question. Come on! She doesn’t know how to play the game at all. <br /><br />And here I feel compelled to ask my invisible friend: ‘‘What game? Where is the game?’’. Most of it consists of Tella walking around lavish places and talking to random people. <br /><br />How exciting. *yawns*<br /><br />Also, was the writing always so annoying and purple-infused? All I know is that I <i>devoured</i> the first book and this one I couldn’t wait to close. I kid you not, this story is made of 90% of descriptions and 10% of action. It’s sad, really.<br /><br />Oh and am I the only one who finds all of the male characters/love interests to have ridiculously similar personalities? Ms. Garber sure is into alpha males and Mr. Darcy variants. <br /><br />I was ready to love this book. This is heartbreaking, especially since I have a feeling there will be more books. <br /><br /><a href="https://hitormissbooks.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/c/LolaReviewer" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a>Twitter</a> | <a>Instagram</a> | <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/105021852309973899120/posts" rel="nofollow noopener">Google+</a> | <a href="https://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/hit-miss-books-12564715" rel="nofollow noopener">Bloglovin’</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="9601171577469361176" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2420444271" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2420444271" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2420444271?book_show_action=true">Jun 13, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=magical-fantasy">magical-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=audio-books">audio-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=reread">reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2019">read-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2018">read-2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2420444271" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5899708292520694244"><b>Do you know what is an absolute magical delicious delight?! THIS BOOK.</b> There is no hope for me btw, I am completely <i>gone</i>. I'm just so in love with this world, these characters, the twisty plots of magic and mind games and darkness and glitter...it is EVERYTHING. It just captures me so much! Coupled with gorgeous writing that makes you feel like you, too, get to experience Caraval?!<br/><br/>10000% all my affections are YOURS, little book, I'm ready to be destroyed for the finale. Who needs calmness anyway</span>
  <span id="freeText5899708292520694244" style="display:none"><b>Do you know what is an absolute magical delicious delight?! THIS BOOK.</b> There is no hope for me btw, I am completely <i>gone</i>. I'm just so in love with this world, these characters, the twisty plots of magic and mind games and darkness and glitter...it is EVERYTHING. It just captures me so much! Coupled with gorgeous writing that makes you feel like you, too, get to experience Caraval?!<br /><br />10000% all my affections are YOURS, little book, I'm ready to be destroyed for the finale. Who needs calmness anyway. [chokes on a laugh and dies]<br /><br /><b>+ I was really excited that we get to have another game of Caraval!</b><br />This time it's set in a different town, different rules, different stakes = but it's still so intoxicatingly mysterious and twisty. This is like one of my favourite Slytherin books. NO ONE is being straightforward. It's all double-crossing the double crossed and outwitting someone who's already playing tricks on you. Who's lying???? Who's who they say they are??? WE DON'T GET TO KNOW. I freaking love this.<br /><br /><b>+ It's narrated by Tella this time.</b><br />Thank you, lifesaver, because holy heck, Tella is AWESOME. (And I won't lie lmao, Scarlett was so whiny and such a damsel in book one that I nearly broke a plate and ate through a brick wall.) Tella is refreshingly <i>herself</i>. She kisses boys without a care and wears murderously gorgeous dresses and is unapologetic. Also she doesn't judge Scarlett for being an opposite and <i>Scarlett doesn't judge her</i>. TheSE SISTERS. THANK YOU. <b>And I also loved how Tella is caught between playing games and actually fiercely caring about things.</b> The whole book she's like: "I dO NOT LOVE" while, ya know, furiously loving so so many people.<br /><br />YOU'RE GOING TO GET HURT, TELLA, AND I'LL CRY WITH YOU.<br /><br /><b>+ The sisters!! Can we !! flail over the !! sister bonds!!</b><br /> Family is like such a huge theme for these books! Scarlett would do anything for Tella and Tella would do anything for Scarlett. AND her mother! Like Tella just really wants to find her long-lost-mother. And also the fact that Scarlett/Tella are survivors of abuse and they like <i>support each other and listen</i> is really really awesome afjdkslad. <b>Bring me all the sister stories.</b> Reminds me that I'd sell all my sisters for a grape but I DON'T CARE. I APPRECIATE THE FICTIONAL ONES.<br /><br /><b>+ Okay but all the boys?! They were beautiful and also probably evil.</b><br />I love it. This is like the <i>right</i> way to write devious and dark boys...it's not all alpha/abusive/relationships. (THANK YOOOOU.) It's mind games and sinister magic and otherworldly powers and manipulation. Livin' for the Slytherins here. LIVIN FOR IT. <b>Also I totally loved Dante, who works in Caraval but maybe/maybe doesn't love Tella.</b> Their relationship is so love/hate and trust/distrust, but it played out so well. And infuriatingly. I will sCREAM a little, but it's ok.<br /><br />Also Jacks was a freaking nightmare but also so interesting. Also he ate a lot of apples and was so pale he was nearly blue and 100% an otherworldly demon. But why so many apples Jacks. I have eaten pears for like 3 months straight and now can't touch them again. Do not ruin apple pie for yourself, you dumb son, look at me looking out for the villains. I can't even.<br /><br /><b>+ THE MAGIC!!</b><br />This time we have cursed cards and Fates who are trying to be let free. And also there's the eternal question of: WHO IS LEGEND. (I knooooow now afjdklafds I KNOW!!!) And every question and mystery and complicated messy subplot was tied up so <i>gorgeously</i>.<br /><br /><b>I'M JUST A WHOLE PLATE OF GUSHING ADORATION RIGHT NOW. UGH. LOOK AT ME GO.</b><br /><br /><b>+ And the ending?!</b><br />Both satisfying and torturous. I want morrrre and I'm slightly suffocating with the need to find out what happens next. I think (I heard?!) both Scarlett and Tella will narrate the next one and I'm !!! excited!! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Although I lowkey think Scarlett is a brat for knowing she's in love with Julian, but also seeking out her other fiancé?!?!?!? why???? AnD DANTE AND JULIAN ARE BROS I LOVE THIS. I want more of their backstory stat. Dante...you horrid little beautiful snake off for the throne. Go Legend. I think I love him too, Tella, someone save us. 😭❤️❤️ <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br /><b>ALL IN ALL: This was an enthralling read of magic and puzzles, with the most intoxicating plot and characters I just couldn't get enough of.</b> I was glued to this page. My eyeballs are in LOVE with the gorgeously lush writing. The gowns! The flowers! The jewels! The richness dripping off the page in perfect descriptions! GAH. Everything about this caught my heart.<br /><br /><br /><i>** Quotes taken from the ARC**</i><br /><br /><blockquote>Scarlett was Tella's person -- the one someone in the world whom Tella could always count on. Tella might not have believed in falling love, but she had literally bet her life that Scarlett loved her. Tella would destroy the world before she allowed anything to happen to her sister.</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>Every dish imaginable, from honeycomb towers with edible flowers to a candied pig with an apple in its mouth, was present. There were miniature fruit trees growing out of chocolate-dipped plumbs and brown-sugar-glazed peaches. Wedges of cheese peeking out of miniature treasure chests made of pastry. Upside-down turtle shells filled with soup. Finger sandwiches shaped like actual fingers. colourful plates of salted pink and red radishes. Water with lavender bubbles, and peach-coloured wine with berries at the bottom of the glass.</blockquote><br /><br /><br />*:·ﾟ✧*:·ﾟ✧*:·ﾟ✧*:·ﾟ✧<br /><b>READ 2 | May 2019</b><br /><br />Because this book, which actually is my favourite of life, fully deserved a reread before Finale...(and shh yes I realise I'm <i>late</i> and Finale has been out for weeks, but hey...I did enjoy just savouring this!) Honestly it's the type of book that breaks my soul open with its sheer gorgeousness, ability to make me feel, and utter charming and wickedly reckless high-stack plot, that just makes <i>me</i> want to write better. <b>I love love love this book.</b> ARGH I LOVE TELLA AND DANTE. And the stakes are so high in this one, it's impossible not to lose your heartbeat.<br /><br />(And the audio is amazing! I definitely recommend it!)<br /><br />am in love. that is all. this book is pure magic, pure writing skill, and pure creative genius.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5899708292520694244" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2447979755" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2447979755" />
    <a title="High Lady of The Night Court" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/62560505-high-lady-of-the-night-court"><img alt="High Lady of The Night Court" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1556501727p2/62560505.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2447979755?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="High Lady of The Night Court" class="user" itemprop="url" name="High Lady of The Night Court" href="/user/show/62560505-high-lady-of-the-night-court">High Lady of The Night Court</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/62560505-high-lady-of-the-night-court?shelf=fantasy-read">fantasy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2447979755" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3548898268985904999"><i>
  <b>"The air tasted like wonder. Like candied butterfly wings caught in sugared spiderwebs, and drunken peaches coated in luck."</b>
</i><br/><br/>This game is a dream wrapped in nightmares, yet to some it is a nightmare wrapped in a dream, it is deceptive, it is beautiful, it is addictive and yet it is the one thing that can break your mind before it breaks your heart, or maybe even both at the very same moment without you ever realising it. It is hatred and love and happiness and sorrow. There are more players i</span>
  <span id="freeText3548898268985904999" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"The air tasted like wonder. Like candied butterfly wings caught in sugared spiderwebs, and drunken peaches coated in luck."</b>
</i><br /><br />This game is a dream wrapped in nightmares, yet to some it is a nightmare wrapped in a dream, it is deceptive, it is beautiful, it is addictive and yet it is the one thing that can break your mind before it breaks your heart, or maybe even both at the very same moment without you ever realising it. It is hatred and love and happiness and sorrow. There are more players in this game than we imagined, but this time they might just be real. Beings of monsters and magic filled with a desired for something beyond our knowledge. <br /> But just keep in mind, it’s only a game… or is it.<br /><br /><br />In this sequel to the beguiling story of Caraval, Tella will risk her life to find her mother who abandoned her and her sister when they were kids. In order to find her mother, Tella reaches out to people who might just be more danger then they’re worth, but love makes people do crazy things and this time it might just result in her death. She’s putting her life on the line for a mother whose true identity might just change her perspective on everything she’s stepping into and in her attempts to find her long lost mother she might lose her sister who risked her very sanity to find her in the last game.<br /><br />I absolutely love the fact that Tella is always so honest with herself and knows what she wants and what she’ll do to get it. Anyone else would tell themselves lies to cover up their true feelings to justify what they are or are not feeling, but Tella will think to herself that she knows she shouldn’t want something but she happens to want it so she will hold herself back or will give into it. She will let let herself indulge in her desires whenever she can but will ignore all comforts if it means doing what she has to do. I like that she will finds bits of happiness and satisfaction whenever she can, however dire the circumstances, because time may be endless but life is not.<br /><br />I love the descriptions of everything throughout the book. The concept of Caraval in itself is so dreamlike and magical that the near poetic descriptions of people, places, and thoughts adds to the beauty and mystery that is Caraval. And I swear I can read the clues in this game a million times and not get bored of them, because those words are put together like a tailor weaves cloth, each thread put together in the most perfect way possible to make every thread seem impeccably melded into the one before it in the most seamless way possible. The writing of this book is amazing and I will always look forward to Stephanie Garber’s books. The characters in this book are mind blowing in their own complexity and the nature of Caraval will make you question whether you really know the person or just the role they’re playing.<br /><br />I would have liked a more definitive ending but the open end of the book maintains the mysterious charm of Caraval and left me entranced because the endless possibilities of where this story could go is mesmerising. And to no one’s surprise this book, just like the last one, leaves me even further obsessed with this series. I figured out nearly every plot twist in this book, but now I think the frustration of having figured out a lot more than the protagonist adds to the infinite mystery of this concept of Caraval. I can’t wait for the finale of the series of this enchanting world filled with stories begging to be told. 5 stars again!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3548898268985904999" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2138878895" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2138878895" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2138878895?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781250095336" href="/book/show/33645809-legendary">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2138878895" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4051677783605670708"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1527312709i/25599017._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>ARC provided by Flatiron in exchange for an honest review.</i><br/><br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1899590130' rel='nofollow noopener'>Caraval</a> ★★★★<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“But the best villains are the ones you secretly like, and my nana always said Legend was the villain in Caraval.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>I know that <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1899590130' rel='nofollow noopener'>Caraval</a> was a super polarizing read last year when it released, but I fell on the side of totally loving. From the game, to the mystery, to the lyrical writing, to the compelling characters, I couldn’t get enough. I devoured it in two sittings and never wanted to stop the reading experie</span>
  <span id="freeText4051677783605670708" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1527312709i/25599017._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>ARC provided by Flatiron in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1899590130" rel="nofollow noopener">Caraval</a> ★★★★<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“But the best villains are the ones you secretly like, and my nana always said Legend was the villain in Caraval.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I know that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1899590130" rel="nofollow noopener">Caraval</a> was a super polarizing read last year when it released, but I fell on the side of totally loving. From the game, to the mystery, to the lyrical writing, to the compelling characters, I couldn’t get enough. I devoured it in two sittings and never wanted to stop the reading experience. And guess what? <i>Legendary</i> was no different. <br><br>In <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1899590130" rel="nofollow noopener">Caraval</a> we follow Scarlett and watch her run away from her home, and her abusive father, so that she can try to rescue her sister, Donatella, by winning the magical game of Caraval. Well, immediately after the outcome from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1899590130" rel="nofollow noopener">Caraval</a>, <i>Legendary</i> picks right up. Except this time, we follow Donatella, and she has stumbled on her own very own mystery and her very own game. And forget everything you think you learned in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1899590130" rel="nofollow noopener">Caraval</a>, because this trilogy takes a completely new approach, with completely new twists and turns, in <i>Legendary</i>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Legend has chosen you to play a game that may change your destiny.<br>In honor of Empress Elantine’s 75th birthday,<br>Caraval will visit the streets of Valenda for six magical nights.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The invitations are distributed and a brand-new game of Caraval is going to begin, in a brand-new empire that is ruled by a very powerful empress. And this time Tella has decided to play so that she too has a chance to locate someone who has disappeared from her and Scarlett’s lives, their mother. Paloma was truly a woman of mystery, but we are able to see a few flashbacks that Tella has of her mother, along with a few of the keepsakes that Tella has kept all these years. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“For it was also said the Prince of Hearts was not capable of love, because his heart had stopped beating long ago. Only one person could make it beat again: his one true love. They said his kiss had been fatal to all but her—his only weakness—and as he’d sought her, he’d left a trail of corpses.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>We also get to see that a magical card prophesied that Tella would be a victim of unrequited love for her entire life. So, a ring that appears to be more than just a ring, and a card (think Tarot cards) that Tella took against her mother’s will, is all she has as clues. That is, until she meets someone who knows much more about that particular card, and the entire Deck of Destiny. And Tella ends up trying to win Caraval for this new stranger, for her mother, for her heart, for her life, and for Legend himself. Because the only way Tella will ever see her mother again is to win this game. <br><br>This book also had a bit more romance than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1899590130" rel="nofollow noopener">Caraval</a>, but I was completely living for it. And I’m still living for it, honestly. And like, we are maybe about to get a love triangle and I’m still totally here for it. And some of these scenes were legit 11/10, and I completely recommend. Also, I’m still swooning over Dante. But I also can’t stop thinking about Jacks and love that good angst. Be still, my heart.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ve never wanted to be someone else until that moment I saw him kiss you on the dance floor.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Okay, now I don’t want to gush too hard on you all, but you want to know what this book reminded me of? <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1654767570" rel="nofollow noopener">The Cruel Prince</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2132083151" rel="nofollow noopener">The Wicked King</a> by Holly Black. And chapter thirteen was such a work of art. Probably the best chapter I’ve read in any book in all of 2018. <br><br>So, why did I end up giving this four stars and not five with glowing sentences like the paragraph above this one? With so many twists and turns throughout this book, all of which blindsided me and made me fall more and more in love, the ending ended up being so predictable. Like, to the point that I thought it couldn’t be real, and that the epilogue was going to pull the wool from my eyes. But no, the disappointment just stayed. Which is so sad, because this book was so good, and such a treat to read in every single way, but the ending just made this amazing book really end on a bad note. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Tella would destroy the world before she allowed anything to happen to her sister.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Also, there wasn’t as much of a positive sibling emphasis in this book. Like, Tella was 100% committed to Scarlett, and we know from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1899590130" rel="nofollow noopener">Caraval</a> that Scarlett was 100% committed to Tella, but <i>Legendary</i> didn’t do anything to help enforce that percentage. Scarlett was honestly kind of a hot mess in this book, from start to (especially) end. I pray that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2403951045" rel="nofollow noopener">Finale</a> is either entirely in Tella’s point of view or it switches between Scarlett and Tella’s point of view. I don’t think I can deal with another solo Scarlett book after her actions in <i>Legendary</i>. <br><br>But overall, I really did love reading this. Again, I know not everyone does, but I just love Stephanie Garber’s writing and purple prose so much. I completely connect with it, and it completely immerses. I always feel like I’m there for all six nights of Caraval, in the castles, carriages, balls, and cathedrals. Also, these books and their settings are such aesthetic goals, I swear! Plus, this entire series is such a love letter to morally grey characters! I can’t wait to see how this all wraps up in the last book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2403951045" rel="nofollow noopener">Finale</a>. <br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a> <br><br><i>The quotes above were taken from an ARC and are subject to change upon publication.</i><br><br>Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/13507409-amy" rel="nofollow noopener">Amy</a> at <a href="https://acourtofcrownsandquills.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">A Court of Crowns and Quills</a>! ❤</span>
  <a data-text-id="4051677783605670708" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">
          

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review2138878895">
  <td colspan="2">

<div id="review_2138929136" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2138929136" />
    <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk"><img alt="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597641717p2/66224803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2138929136?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk">Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781250095336" href="/book/show/33645809-legendary">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2138929136" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17245051861126428765"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1529254989ra/25808288.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i> “Every good story needs a villain.<br/>But the best villains are the ones you secretly like.” </i> <br/><br/>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/>First things first: I didn’t really like Caraval. Sure the world was great and the story was pretty cool, but I hated Scarlett and I didn’t really like Julian. <br/>In this book everything is different. <br/>In the last Caraval game Tella was the price you could win by playing Caraval. <br/>But now she’s a player herself and she’s not only playing to win. She’s playing for her own life, the life of her mo</span>
  <span id="freeText17245051861126428765" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1529254989ra/25808288.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> “Every good story needs a villain.<br>But the best villains are the ones you secretly like.” </i> <br><br>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>First things first: I didn’t really like Caraval. Sure the world was great and the story was pretty cool, but I hated Scarlett and I didn’t really like Julian. <br>In this book everything is different. <br>In the last Caraval game Tella was the price you could win by playing Caraval. <br>But now she’s a player herself and she’s not only playing to win. She’s playing for her own life, the life of her mother and the fate of the world. <br>But when confronted with two hard choices - which one will you take? <br>This book was really addictive. It had twists and turns and literally the whole time I didn’t know who to trust and what would be the right choice for Tella. <br>I think this book is a million times better than Caraval. <br><br>Character ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Like I said, I hated Scarlett. But Tella... I loved her from the start. It started with her little girl dreams of rescuing princes (not being rescued). She was brave, strong and so intelligent. She’s definitely one of my favorite characters now. <br>I liked the way she always tried to see who’s lying and who’s honest, who to trust and distrust. She always tried to see the right paths and how she wanted the game to end. <br>But that’s just not possible in this world. <br>The next character I found pretty entertaining is Jacks. He was cruel, he was mean and still he was so much more interesting than everyone else. <br>He was so unpredictable and you never knew what he thought and what he would do. <br>I liked this part of him. <br>Next to Jacks there’s also Dante. I didn’t really remember much of him in Caraval, but I remembered that he was a handsome mean guy. And even though Dante and Tella had huge chemistry, I still had the feeling he wasn’t the right person for her. But still, the tension was so so so sweet. <br>And I need to be honest with you, in my imagination, with the tattoos and all, Dante is really a handsome devil. <br>And I liked that. <br>I like characters that no one really can shove into a role. He’s not the hero, the good guy of this story. But he’s also not the villain, the bad guy. He’s something in between. <br>Then, we get to my least favorite person in this story, Scarlett. I was so annoyed every time she appeared in this book. I just don’t like her, I can’t stand her. <br>And I have the same feelings for Julian. <br>But all in all the characters really did improve with the second book. <br>Especially because the main character was now an awesome female that can kick some ass.<br><br>World ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>I was fascinated with the world in Caraval. <br>It felt magical and I wished there were circuses and games like that. <br>I wish there was some magic in our world ✨<br>This time we’re not on the island of the first games. This time we’re in a big city and there are new characters we get to meet. <br>This time it even feels more magical, more twisted and a bit dark. <br><br>Relationships ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><i> “I think I’d like you even if you were the villain.” </i> <br>Oh man, the whole time I wasn’t really sure if I could choose a love interest if I was Tella. <br>On the one hand I did like Dante and his arrogant but loyal way. But on the other hand I always distrust him. I always had a bad feeling with him. <br>When looking at Jacks and Tella, I never had this distrust. And why is that so? Because he told her from the start that he’s a cruel, emotionless monster that’ll make the world suffer. He never acted differently and that kind of made him sympathetic? <br>Sounds weird and super strange, but what can I do. <br>Next to this undecided love interest there is the love between Scarlett and Tella. I know there are sisters and all, but Scarlett was so so annoying and her stupid secretiveness was even worse. <br>But all in all I was satisfied with the love story in this book, even though I couldn’t decide which side I would be on. <br>(But then even if I knew, I wouldn’t tell you, because that would be a spoiler 😝). <br><br>Writing style ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Oh well, the writing style the author has isn’t the best or the prettiest, but it was really addictive and beautifully descriptive. <br>I liked that the author not only improved in the parts of characters and relationships, she also improved her writing, the story and in some way the world building. <br>So, if you hated/didn’t like/we’re unsure about Caraval, try out Legendary. <br>It’s really better than the first book. <br><br>Reread Nr. 1 ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>I changed my rating from four to five stars, because I reread this book and it was still so addictive and entertaining. Definitely a good thing for a book. <br>Can’t wait to read Finale ✨<br><br>_____________________________________________________<br><br>My friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/52491901" rel="nofollow noopener">Lena ♥️</a> told me this book is absolutely awesome, so I’m gonna read it on my road trip 🚗📖<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1529146778ra/25799274.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="17245051861126428765" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17159277723934797754">okay, not to be dramatic but i would bargain my soul to every one of the fates to be able to live in a world where caraval games existed.<br/><br/>there is nothing quite like the amazement and sensational wonder of these books. i just want to crawl into the pages and spend the rest of my days enthralled by the legendary magic of this story. i will admit this was much slower and more character driven than ‘caraval’ but the enchantment was just as present. i love stories that make me second guess what i kno</span>
  <span id="freeText17159277723934797754" style="display:none">okay, not to be dramatic but i would bargain my soul to every one of the fates to be able to live in a world where caraval games existed.<br /><br />there is nothing quite like the amazement and sensational wonder of these books. i just want to crawl into the pages and spend the rest of my days enthralled by the legendary magic of this story. i will admit this was much slower and more character driven than ‘caraval’ but the enchantment was just as present. i love stories that make me second guess what i know and think, and this captivated me from the first pages (it picks up immediately where the first book ends). and rather than being just a simple caraval game, everything gets so much more complicated - the stakes are higher, new forces are in play, and the truth is more hidden than the identity of legend himself. this was truly an experience and cant wait to see how the story ends in the next book! <br /><br /><b>
  <i>5 stars</i>
</b></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1857570538?book_show_action=true">Dec 30, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8472395-alyssa?shelf=2018-releases">2018-releases</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1857570538" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11140480251540231823">Meehhh. What a disappointment.<br/><br/><br/>***<a href='http://eaterofbooks.blogspot.com/2018/07/review-legendary-by-stephanie-garber.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Review posted on The Eater of Books! blog</a>***<br/><br/>Legendary by Stephanie Garber<br/>Book Two of the Caraval series<br/>Publisher: Flatiron Books<br/>Publication Date: May 29, 2018<br/>Rating: 3 stars<br/>Source: eARC from NetGalley<br/><br/>Summary (from Goodreads):<br/><br/>A heart to protect. A debt to repay. A game to win.<br/><br/>After being swept up in the magical world of Caraval, Donatella Dragna has finally escaped her father and saved her sister Scarlett from a disastrous arranged marriage. The girls should be ce</span>
  <span id="freeText11140480251540231823" style="display:none">Meehhh. What a disappointment.<br><br><br>***<a href="http://eaterofbooks.blogspot.com/2018/07/review-legendary-by-stephanie-garber.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Review posted on The Eater of Books! blog</a>***<br><br>Legendary by Stephanie Garber<br>Book Two of the Caraval series<br>Publisher: Flatiron Books<br>Publication Date: May 29, 2018<br>Rating: 3 stars<br>Source: eARC from NetGalley<br><br>Summary (from Goodreads):<br><br>A heart to protect. A debt to repay. A game to win.<br><br>After being swept up in the magical world of Caraval, Donatella Dragna has finally escaped her father and saved her sister Scarlett from a disastrous arranged marriage. The girls should be celebrating, but Tella isn’t yet free. She made a desperate bargain with a mysterious criminal, and what Tella owes him no one has ever been able to deliver: Caraval Master Legend’s true name.<br><br>The only chance of uncovering Legend’s identity is to win Caraval, so Tella throws herself into the legendary competition once more—and into the path of the murderous heir to the throne, a doomed love story, and a web of secrets…including her sister's. Caraval has always demanded bravery, cunning, and sacrifice. But now the game is asking for more. If Tella can’t fulfill her bargain and deliver Legend’s name, she’ll lose everything she cares about—maybe even her life. But if she wins, Legend and Caraval will be destroyed forever.<br><br>Welcome, welcome to Caraval...the games have only just begun.<br><br>What I Liked:<br><br>I'm actually a bit disappointed by this book, which is of course very surprise given how much I loved Caraval, and given how much everyone has loved Legendary. I felt so meh about this book while reading it, and when I finished it, I was left with a rather sour taste in my mouth. Definitely not what you would want to feel after reading a supposed masterpiece. But these things happen.<br><br>Caraval followed Scarlett Dragna, who entered Caraval in order to save her younger sister Donnatella. Legendary follows Tella, who enters Caraval in order to save her and Scarlett's mother Paloma, who has been missing for years. Paloma is trapped in a card of the Deck of Destiny, a cursed deck of cards that contains the Fates. If the Fates are released, chaos will ensue (or something like that). If Legend gets the Deck, he could gain the powers of all of the Fates in the Deck. In order to save her mother, Tella must find the Deck of Destiny. In order to uphold her bargain with a mysterious criminal who gave her information about her mother, Tella must give the criminal Legend's true identity. Tella has neither of those things, and so she must enter Caraval and win - so that she will receive the ultimate prize from Legend. It's a tricky game that Tella is playing, and it is not without consequences - or sacrifices.<br><br>In the first half of the book, I was pretty engrossed in the story. I wasn't totally sold on the whole finding-my-mother thing, but I was intrigued, and I liked Tella. I liked seeing Scarlett and Julian, though I hated the unnecessary drama (more on that below). I looooved Dante's appearances. I even loved Jacks' ridiculous, cruel self. The first half of the book was so fascinating.<br><br>I liked Tella for the most part. In book one, I pretty much hated her and branded her the most selfish, unworthy sister ever. But I liked her in this book. She is bold and uninhibited, and while she seemed selfish in Caraval, she seems more selfless in this book. It's clear that she loves her sister, but is very guarded. She is selfless when it comes to Paloma, which is how this book came to be. Finding her mother is so important to Tella.<br><br>I adored Dante and his wicked, charming self. I actually didn't totally care for him in book one, but he's so swoony and magical in this book. And not just in a love interest kind of way - the game of Caraval would not be the same without his presence. He's a charming devil, but he's also kind and sweet. He has a commanding presence about him and he has a way of popping up whenever he is needed (and whenever he isn't). <br><br>There are many Scarlett/Julian cameos which I appreciate, though I wish they were all happy cameos showing Scarlett and Julian helplessly in love. I guess that will have to wait until Finale. Still, I'm glad that Julian and Scarlett are part of this book, and an important part.<br><br>I liked the Dante/Tella romance, but there wasn't nearly enough. The author teased with this romance.<br><br>Once I reached the second half of the book, I was kind of finished with it all. I'll talk about all of my dislikes next. I can't even say I liked the ending.<br><br>What I Did Not Like:<br><br>Ugh, where do I even begin? I just felt so meh about this book at the halfway mark and beyond. What went wrong, you might ask? I have no idea. <br><br>I was never truly sold on the whole I-must-find-my-mother plot. It seemed forced and contrived, like the author desperately needed a good reason to bring back Caraval for a second time in a short period (like The Hunger Games), and so she grasped at straws and came up with Scarlett and Tella's missing mother. I just never bought into that plot. It didn't feel important.<br><br>I didn't care for the barely-there tease of a romance that was Dante/Tella. I loved Dante. I liked Tella. I loved Dante/Tella. I didn't love the lack of kisses and swoon.<br><br>And the implicated love triangle - for both Tella and Scarlett! Like two completely separate love triangles going on! What the heck! I thought Julian/Scarlett was a done deal but apparently not. You know what I hate? When girls want to make their man jealous and so they flirt with someone else. Or go find their ex. And they call it "exploring their options" or some bull***t and they want to bring about some competition between their man and the ex/side man. For real? This isn't cute. There's nothing wrong with dating. But there IS something wrong when you claim you love someone and yet you go look for your ex or another man just to make the man you love jealous, or some bull***. That's playing games and it's maddening. I'm talking about Scarlett.<br><br>Oh but Tella is embroiled in her own love triangle, don't you worry. I know she is in love with Dante by the end of the story, and I know he loves her, but there is another guy that seems to be in love with Tella and noooooooo thank you. I actually LOVE this character and I wouldn't mind a Tella/This Character pairing IF Dante had never existed. Meaning, This Character as a love interest is so unnecessary. Why though. Why.<br><br>Speaking of unnecessary, let's talking about all the unnecessary drama that is in this book. I already talked about Scarlett's bull**** that she's pulling with Julian, but I hate that she also let's so many factors bring down their relationship. She takes every little thing as a reason not to trust him. She knows who he is, what his role in Caraval is, and yet she whines about it all the time. I liked Scarlett in the first book. But she really got on my nerves in this book. And as much as I liked seeing her and Julian in this book, I would appreciated it more if there was less drama and more swoon. More of them working together as a couple, rather than Scarlett acting like a crazy girlfriend who runs off to her exes every time she believes something about her man (to put the situation in modern terms; Scarlett technically never runs to any exes, but hopefully you understand the picture I'm trying to paint). The drama is just so unnecessary. But I guess it's middle-book drama?<br><br>I think this is part of my frustration with YA these days - the drama is so unnecessary, and sequels tend to suck. In adult romance, a book is a standalone and the story is done within that one book. Thank goodness.<br><br>The ending of this book is not a happy ending. For anyone.<br><br>Would I Recommend It:<br><br>Honestly, this is one of those books where you have to read it yourself. Decide for yourself. 99% of the people who read this book love it, so what do I know? I felt so meh while reading at least half of this book. And the ending made me so sour. Not just because of the obvious love triangles, but because of the drama, and the cliffhanger, and it was just so stupid.<br><br>But again, decide for yourself. I would say that if you're on the fence, maybe just stop with the first book. Wait until the third book publishes and binge-read the series. Or just stop with Caraval. Caraval had a lovely ending and you can imagine an epilogue of Scarlett and Julian 40 years down the road, happily ever after. No need to read about unnecessary drama. <br><br>Rating:<br><br>2.5 stars -&gt; rounded up to 3 stars. Perhaps I'm being generous, and maybe I just really wanted to love the book. I was so excited about it and so prepared to love it like I did Caraval. But I'm glad I didn't buy this book because I would have regretted. I'm happy to have had the opportunity to review it (I was supposed to post this review two months ago, whoops), but I would have regretted spending the money on it. I will read Finale but it'll be a library request from me.<br><br><br><br><strong>Pre-read squees:</strong><br><br>MEEEEEEE, I WANT IT!!!!!!!!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410457450ra/11110018.gif" width="390" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436052962ra/15412966.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436053035ra/15413003.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="11140480251540231823" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2548668384" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2548668384" />
    <a title="Chelsea Humphrey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47207032-chelsea-humphrey"><img alt="Chelsea Humphrey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585613513p2/47207032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2548668384?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea Humphrey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea Humphrey" href="/user/show/47207032-chelsea-humphrey">Chelsea Humphrey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47207032-chelsea-humphrey?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2548668384" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14690817940632473388">Wow, this was so much more enjoyable the second time through, so much that I’ve bumped my rating up a full star. I love the narrator and am finally ready for the Finale!<br/><br/>********************<br/><br/>I'm clearly in the minority with my middle of the road rating here, but I just couldn't push it any higher than 3 stars. I read an arc of <i>Caraval</i> back in August of 2016 and fell in love with the characters, the world, and the game itself. The story was one where I couldn't put it down, so much so that I read i</span>
  <span id="freeText14690817940632473388" style="display:none">Wow, this was so much more enjoyable the second time through, so much that I’ve bumped my rating up a full star. I love the narrator and am finally ready for the Finale!<br /><br />********************<br /><br />I'm clearly in the minority with my middle of the road rating here, but I just couldn't push it any higher than 3 stars. I read an arc of <i>Caraval</i> back in August of 2016 and fell in love with the characters, the world, and the game itself. The story was one where I couldn't put it down, so much so that I read it all in a single day while traveling home from the beach. I cried as loudly as possible in any direction I could for people to pick it up and read it; Garber created a strong fantasy world that was clean and age appropriate, and I applauded her for doing so in a way that was still appealing to teens. Still, years later, I cannot recommend <i>Caraval</i> highly enough, and while I see why it was stretched out to be a trilogy, I also could have seen it ending slightly altered and being a strong stand alone.<br /><br />I'm trying to pinpoint exactly why <i>Legendary</i> didn't work as well for me. It may be because this story felt choppily tied to the first, almost as if it was an afterthought to continue in this direction rather than naturally flowing from the first book. It could also be the fact that I simply didn't connect with Tella's narration as well as I did with Scarlett's in the first book, possibly because I don't like her as much. <i>*shrugs*</i> Whatever the case, and as negative as this all sounds, I still did consider this a positive reading experience; I typically struggle with middle installments in trilogies and this one was fast paced and suspenseful from beginning to end. It's an easy read, one that almost reads itself, and while we're still left with questions, it was fun experiencing a totally different plot than the first and pondering whether the information we receive at the end is indeed true or simply left to throw us off our game until next year.<br /><br />Garber is clearly a talented author; her writing is easy to connect with and appealing to a wide age range, and while I didn't love <i>Legendary</i> as much as I did the previous novel, I'm still looking forward to <i>Finale</i> in 2019. <br /><br /><i>*Buddy read with my sister Irina. &lt;3</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14690817940632473388" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15693464569236385022">First off, there’s another book, right? Because this book left me with too many unanswered questions! More than book one... so it’s a bit tricky for me here because if there’s another book, then this one was hella great, but if this is the last book then I’m just too flustered to think!<br/><br/>I’m just going to go ahead and say that the world that Stephanie Garber has created is freaking cool and amazing. I thought Tella was a decent character, although I did like Scarlett more.<br/><br/>As with Julian, I really </span>
  <span id="freeText15693464569236385022" style="display:none">First off, there’s another book, right? Because this book left me with too many unanswered questions! More than book one... so it’s a bit tricky for me here because if there’s another book, then this one was hella great, but if this is the last book then I’m just too flustered to think!<br /><br />I’m just going to go ahead and say that the world that Stephanie Garber has created is freaking cool and amazing. I thought Tella was a decent character, although I did like Scarlett more.<br /><br />As with Julian, I really liked Dante. Stephanie can write some great males! Even the new character Jacks was incredibly intriguing. I love the mystery behind the curtains, because I never know what's going to be revealed to me. Who is Legend? Where is Legend? What is Legend? Do I know? I think I know! These books really do feel like a game, and a game I enjoy playing.<br /><br />So again if this is the last book, then I’m sort of pissed lol. But if it’s not then bravo, bravo, bravo. If you want a great place to escape, then try to find your way through Caraval and live through Garber's gorgeous writing!<br /><br />Review on my blog <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://literarydust.wordpress.com/2018/03/16/review-legendary/">https://literarydust.wordpress.com/20...</a></span>

<div id="review_1900430137" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1900430137" />
    <a title="Jiana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana"><img alt="Jiana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540380229p2/10502567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1900430137?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jiana" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana">Jiana</a>
      </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3437796029938569674"><b>I can't help but enjoy being swept away by the magic that is Legend!</b><br/><br/>I can't give away anything for fear of spoilers but I'll be honest and say that I actually loved this second book even more than the first one.   <span id="freeText3437796029938569674" style="display:none"><b>I can't help but enjoy being swept away by the magic that is Legend!</b><br /><br />I can't give away anything for fear of spoilers but I'll be honest and say that I actually loved this second book even more than the first one. She is feisty, loyal and quite formidable. It's dark and magical and absolutely mesmerizing. The images I painted in my mind as I read the book added so much to my overall enjoyment of the story. I can't wait to see what magic Garber conjures up for book 3!</span>

<div id="review_1896106015" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1896106015" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1896106015?book_show_action=true">May 23, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K. Elizabeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K. Elizabeth" href="/user/show/17568354-k-elizabeth">K. Elizabeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17568354-k-elizabeth?shelf=cover-love">cover-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17568354-k-elizabeth?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17568354-k-elizabeth?shelf=imaginative">imaginative</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17568354-k-elizabeth?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17568354-k-elizabeth?shelf=memorable-characters">memorable-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17568354-k-elizabeth?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17568354-k-elizabeth?shelf=original-idea">original-idea</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17568354-k-elizabeth?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17568354-k-elizabeth?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17568354-k-elizabeth?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1896106015" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9967071396052133135"><i>Re-read in 2019</i>: I still freaking love this book. It's incredibly magical.<br/>_________________________________________<br/>**Warning: this text may contain spoilers** ★ 4.5 / 5 ★<br/><br/>What a magical, whimsical, lovely second book to this series! Stephanie Garber has a story-telling gift and ya’ll are missing out if you haven’t already read Caraval.<br/><br/>As someone who loved Caraval, I was nervous to start Legendary, because often times I’m disappointed by the sequel in a series—well, folks, that wasn’t the case her</span>
  <span id="freeText9967071396052133135" style="display:none"><i>Re-read in 2019</i>: I still freaking love this book. It's incredibly magical.<br />_________________________________________<br />**Warning: this text may contain spoilers** ★ 4.5 / 5 ★<br /><br />What a magical, whimsical, lovely second book to this series! Stephanie Garber has a story-telling gift and ya’ll are missing out if you haven’t already read Caraval.<br /><br />As someone who loved Caraval, I was nervous to start Legendary, because often times I’m disappointed by the sequel in a series—well, folks, that wasn’t the case here! This book was so marvelous that I didn’t mind reading in Tella’s perspective (I say that because I loved Scarlett’s POV); in fact, I might even say that I preferred it. But honestly, I love both Scarlett and Tella; so I’m fine reading in either of their perspectives. It’s books like these that make me wish I had a sister.<br /><br />Because I feel like I haven’t said this enough to my friends today (the ones that would listen): Legendary seriously blew my mind. The writing, of course, was flawless and smooth; it’s practically like butter for your mind (without the unhealthiness). <br /><br />The characters, too, are mysterious and magical and wonderful. I loved getting to know more about Caraval’s actors/actresses; it was a real ride. <br /><br />Okay, so, ehem, Dante is mine (sorry, Tella). I already mentioned that in one of my updates, but I’m repeating myself so people don’t forget. I mean, I liked him in Caraval but I loved him in Legendary. He’s dark and gritty and a walking secret; I can’t wait to learn more about him in book three!<br /><br />Surprisingly, Jacks is a close second, after Dante (of course). When he was introduced to Tella I sensed he was purposefully being presented as this novel's cruel character. I say “purposefully” because when Jacks was introduced I could tell Stephanie Garber was trying to make the reader dislike him … which usually means you’ll end up loving him. So even though I expected to end up liking Jacks, I was pleased how naturally it happened. I also think he’s just playing the villainous role and is good/caring inside. I'd still date him bad or good though.<br /><br />For anyone curious, I took a half-star off because there were some things I suspected early on, which ended up being right. I was hoping it would be a little harder to put things together.<br /><br />Overall, there is so much more I want to write about (like Julian and Scarlett and their cute relationship…and all the other thingssss that were revealed), but because I don’t want to risk giving away more than I might’ve, I’ll stop here. But, let it be known, this is a phenomenal series and I can’t wait for book three.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9967071396052133135" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
